ChargePoint offers a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity to create an all-electric future and a trillion-dollar market.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Join the team that is building the EV charging industry and make your mark on how people and goods will get everywhere they need to go, in any context, for generations to come.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Discover what it's like to help build the fueling network of the future - check out our Engineering Blog.<\u002Fp> \n <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b> Reports To<\u002Fb><\u002Fh3> \n <p> Sr. Operations Manager<\u002Fp> \n <p><b> What You Will Be Doing<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n <p> The logistics and fulfilment manager is responsible for driving projects in the European supply chain in particular on the order to cash processes including, but not limited to, fulfilment processes, warehousing and logistics optimisation and returns processing and handling. You will succeed by analysing current processes and reports, making suggestions to improve and automate where possible to drive change and introducing process and rigour to help scale the business. You will be fundamental to supporting our ambitious growth targets and optimising our processes for growth. This position is located in Europe but you will be working closely with the teams at ChargePoint headquarters in California, Mexico and rest of Europe. This is a highly cross functional role with visibility to global teams and leadership, where you will be expected to wear many hats and own a wide scope of processes as we build the team going forward.<\u002Fp> \n <p><b> Required Qualifications (General)<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n <ul> \n  <li>Serve as subject matter expert for Supply Chain improvement projects including warehousing, fulfilment and RMA<\u002Fli> \n  <li>A strong network in the European logistics industry and experience managing RFP processes for contracting new carriers and expanding capacity<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Deep knowledge of ERP systems, EDI interfaces and applying best practice processes to meet business needs such as spare parts management, support\u002FFSO processes and RMA\u002Freverse logistics processes<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Experienced with identifying improvement opportunities and facilitating the change<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Self-motivated, able to work independently and under pressure, to accomplish tasks on time and with high quality results<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Able to deal with ambiguous environments by exercising independent judgment in methods, techniques and evaluating criteria to obtain the best results. becoming a reality. ChargePoint (NYSE: CHPT) is at the center of this revolution, powering one of the world's leading EV charging networks and a comprehensive set of hardware, software and mobile solutions for every charging need across North America and Europe. We bring together drivers, businesses, automakers, policymakers, utilities and other stakeholders to make e-mobility a global reality.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Since our founding in 2007, ChargePoint has focused solely on making the transition to electric easy for businesses, fleets and drivers. ChargePoint offers a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity to create an all-electric future and a trillion-dollar market.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Join the team that is building the EV charging industry and make your mark on how people and goods will get everywhere they need to go, in any context, for generations to come.<\u002Fp>\n <br> \n <p><\u002Fp> \n <p><b> Job Description<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n <p> We seek the brightest minds from a wide range of disciplines to develop and deliver high-quality, innovative solutions. becoming a reality. ChargePoint (NYSE: CHPT) is at the center of this revolution, powering one of the world's leading EV charging networks and a comprehensive set of hardware, software and mobile solutions for every charging need across North America and Europe. We bring together drivers, businesses, automakers, policymakers, utilities and other stakeholders to make e-mobility a global reality.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Since our founding in 2007, ChargePoint has focused solely on making the transition to electric easy for businesses, fleets and drivers. ChargePoint offers a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity to create an all-electric future and a trillion-dollar market.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Join the team that is building the EV charging industry and make your mark on how people and goods will get everywhere they need to go, in any context, for generations to come.<\u002Fp> \n <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b> What You Will Be Doing<\u002Fb><\u002Fh3> \n <p> You will be part of the product design team that is responsible for the charging station management software solutions  both enterprise as consumer type users. You will regularly attend meetings with customers and will be able to gather feedback on any user experience related issues.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Besides the product teams you will also work with colleagues in our offices in Campbell, Ca and Radstadt, Austria on creating global solutions that span experiences with driver mobile apps, auto in-dash experiences and interactions with charging stations.<\u002Fp> \n <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b> What You Will Bring to ChargePoint<\u002Fb><\u002Fh3> \n <ul>\n  <li>Work on the informational structures (mental models, flows, sitemaps, etc.) based on the research and define the user experience for both existing and future products.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Create UI designs based on our Atomic Design System and review, discuss, and update the components with other designers.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Effectively present and persuasively convey design solutions to team members.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Collaborate with developers (front end, back end, data science) to make sure the implementation of your designs is done right.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Initiate, plan for, and conduct user research (both qualitative and quantitative) and analyze the outcomes with team members and relevant stakeholders.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Contribute, along with other designers, to the longer-term strategy of UX within the organization.<\u002Fli> \n <\u002Ful>\n <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>Requirements<\u002Fb><\u002Fh3> \n <ul>\n  <li>3+ years of work experience in UX\u002FUI Design, in a B2B environment is a plus.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Up to date knowledge of web app technologies and developments.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Experience in working in agile teams.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Experience in (design) tools such as or similar to;
